<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:conserveren.html>conserveren</a> (36220)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">conserver</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:conserveren.html>conserveren</a></strong>

***consolideren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:consolideren.html>consolideren</a> (65581)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:consolideren.html>consolideren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">consolider</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:consolideren.html>consolideren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to consolidate, to strengthen</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">consolidatie</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:consolideren.html>consolideren</a></b>
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">consumption</span>, act of eating or drinking

***cooper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cooper.html>cooper</a> (4689)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">coop</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cooper.html>cooper</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:coopers.html>coopers</a></b>)
</p>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cooper_(profession)" class="extiw" title="w:Cooper (profession)"><a href = vnd.unilang:cooper.html>Cooper</a> (profession)</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cooper_(profession)" class="extiw" title="w:Cooper (profession)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<ol><li>A craftsman who <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> and repairs <a href = vnd.unilang:barrels.html>barrels</a> and similar wooden vessels such as casks, <a href = vnd.unilang:buckets.html>buckets</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:tubs.html>tubs</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stout.html>stout</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>porter</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cooper.html>cooper</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:coopers.html>coopers</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">coopering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">coopered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now  <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To make and repair <a href = vnd.unilang:barrels.html>barrels</a> etc.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cooperage</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">wine <a href = vnd.unilang:cooper.html>cooper</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cooper.html>cooper</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:coopers.html>coopers</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:copen.html>copen</a> (84200)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">cōpon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kaupōną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">caupō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="dum">côpen</strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to buy</li>
<li>to trade</li>
<li>to buy off</li></ol>

***copycat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:copycat.html>copycat</a> (76619)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">copy</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cat</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">former derogatory term for a person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:copycat.html>copycat</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:copycats.html>copycats</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One who imitates or plagiarizes others' work.</li>
<li>A criminal who imitates the crimes of another; specifically, a criminal who commits the same crime, especially a highly-publicized one, that <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> just <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> or recently committed by someone else.
<dl><dd><i>a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:copycat.html>copycat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:strangler.html>strangler</a></i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:copycat.html>copycat</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:copycat.html>copycat</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:copycat.html>copycat</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Imitative; unoriginal.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1997</b>,  “The Atlantic monthly”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"Because of my size, I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a natural leader in <a href = vnd.unilang:junior.html>junior</a> high school. <a href = vnd.unilang:gangs.html>Gangs</a> are the most <b><a href = vnd.unilang:copycat.html>copycat</a></b> of subcultures. It used to be <a href = vnd.unilang:zoot.html>zoot</a> suits; now it's <a href = vnd.unilang:tattoos.html>tattoos</a>. When I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> thirteen, I got a tattoo"</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1997</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:daniel.html>Daniel</a> Miller,  <cite>Capitalism: an ethnographic approach</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">As one executive put it: Now in the beverage market <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> are to a great extent very <b><a href = vnd.unilang:copycat.html>copycat</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2009</b>,  Alan <a href = vnd.unilang:cole.html>Cole</a>,  <cite>Fathering your father: the Zen of fabrication in <a href = vnd.unilang:tang.html>Tang</a> Buddhism</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> that very <b><a href = vnd.unilang:copycat.html>copycat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of "grandfather stealing" that <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> Jinjue's text look like the son of Du Fei's <i>Record</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> as it works to push Du Fei's "father-text" out of the way.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:copycat.html>copycat</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:copycats.html>copycats</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">copycatting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">copycatted</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To act as a <a href="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:copycat.html>copycat</a></a>; to copy in a shameless or derivative way
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b> September 3,  <a href = vnd.unilang:janet.html>Janet</a> Maslin,  “His Girl Friday Meets a Sadistically <a href = vnd.unilang:chic.html>Chic</a> Serial Killer”, in  <cite>New York Times</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2007/09/03/arts/03masl.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In a genre that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> rife with <b>copycatting</b>, Ms. <a href = vnd.unilang:cain.html>Cain</a> deserves some credit for having gotten a potentially interesting new series off the ground.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
